<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спора.html>спор</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-щик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ščik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спорщик.html>спо́рщик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spórščik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спорщик.html>спо́рщика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спорщик.html>спо́рщики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спорщик.html>спо́рщиков</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">спо́рщица</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> debater, disputant</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> argumentative person</li></ol>

***способность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:способность.html>спосо́бность</a> (1489)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:способный.html>спосо́бный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sposóbnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:способность.html>спосо́бность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sposóbnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:способность.html>спосо́бности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:способность.html>спосо́бности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:способность.html>спосо́бностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ability, capability (the quality or state of being able)</li>
<li>faculty</li>
<li>capacity
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">покупа́тельная <a href = vnd.unilang:способность.html>спосо́бность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pokupátelʹnaja sposóbnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">purchasing power</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>talent (often plural)</li>
<li>power</li>
<li>quality</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возможность.html>возмо́жность</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vozmóžnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умение.html>уме́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uménije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:способ.html>спо́соб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spósob</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. </p>

***способствовавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:способствовать.html>спосо́бствовавший</a> (2951)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:способствовать.html>спосо́бствовавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sposóbstvovavšij</span>)
</p>

***спотыкаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спотыкаться.html>спотыка́ться</a> (6890)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тыка́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tykátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with meaning following the corresponding perfective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:споткнуться.html>споткну́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spotknútʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спотыкаться.html>спотыка́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spotykátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:споткнуться.html>споткну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stumble <i>(over)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спотыкаться.html>спотыка́ясь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">idtí <b>spotykájasʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stumble/stagger along</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stumble <i>(over)</i>, to get stuck <i>(on)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slip, to make a mistake
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спотыкаться.html>спотыка́лись</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vy ne raz <b>spotykálisʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">you have slipped more than once</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спохватывавшийся.html>спохва́тывавшийся</a> (16891)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спохватывавшийся.html>спохва́тывавшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spoxvátyvavšijsja</span>)
</p>

***справедливо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:справедливый.html>справедли́во</a> (5197)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справедливый.html>справедли́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spravedlívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справедливый.html>справедли́во</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spravedlívo</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-справедли́во" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)справедли́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-справедли́во" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)справедли́вей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>justly, fairly <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a just or fair manner</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:справедливый.html>справедли́вый</a> (4086)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вда</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ли́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справедливый.html>справедли́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spravedlívyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)справедли́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)справедли́вей</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">справедли́вейший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>just, fair</li>
<li>true, correct</li></ol>

***справить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:справить.html>справить</a> (15544)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>пра́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справить.html>спра́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">správitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справлять.html>справля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to celebrate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справить.html>спра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рождение.html>рожде́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>správitʹ</b> denʹ roždénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to celebrate one's birthday</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справить.html>спра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свадьба.html>сва́дьбу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>správitʹ</b> svádʹbu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to celebrate one's wedding</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to buy <i>(for)</i>, to acquire <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справить.html>спра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жена.html>жене́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шуба.html>шу́бу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>správitʹ</b> žené šúbu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to buy a fur coat for one's wife</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>in expression only</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справить.html>спра́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нужда.html>нужду́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>správitʹ</b> nuždú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do one's business; do the deed</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:справиться.html>спра́виться</a> (2283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справить.html>спра́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">správitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справиться.html>спра́виться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">správitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справляться.html>справля́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to inquire (after, about), to ask (about), to look up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справиться.html>спра́виться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:словарь.html>словаре́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>správitʹsja</b> v slovaré</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to look up (a word) in a dictionary, to consult a dictionary</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to manage, to cope (with), to get the better (of)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справиться.html>спра́виться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:трудный.html>тру́дной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задача.html>зада́чей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>správitʹsja</b> s trúdnoj zadáčej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cope with a difficult task</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справить.html>спра́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">správitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:справлять.html>справля́ть</a> (13339)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справить.html>спра́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">správitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справлять.html>справля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spravljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справить.html>спра́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to celebrate

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справлять.html>справля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свадьба.html>сва́дьбу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spravljátʹ</b> svádʹbu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to celebrate one's wedding</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to buy <i>(for)</i>, to acquire <i>(for)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справлять.html>справля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нужда.html>нужду́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spravljátʹ</b> nuždú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do one's business; do the deed</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="разговорное">разг.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:приводить.html>приводи́ть</a> что-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядок.html>поря́док</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Лукашка <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>вста́в</a>, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:справлять.html>справля́л</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:ружье.html>ружьё</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:справляться.html>справля́ться</a> (6915)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справлять.html>справля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spravljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справляться.html>справля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spravljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справиться.html>спра́виться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to inquire (after, about), to ask (about), to look up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справляться.html>справля́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:словарь.html>словаре́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spravljátʹsja</b> v slovaré</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to look up (a word) in a dictionary, to consult a dictionary</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to manage, to cope (with), to get the better of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справляться.html>справля́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:трудный.html>тру́дной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задача.html>зада́чей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spravljátʹsja</b> s trúdnoj zadáčej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cope with a difficult task</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справлять.html>справля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spravljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справочный.html>спра́вочный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">správočnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> inquiry
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справочный.html>спра́вочное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бюро.html>бюро́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>správočnoje</b> bjuró</i> ― <span class="e-translation">inquiry office; information desk</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справочный.html>спра́вочное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:издание.html>изда́ние</a>; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:справочный.html>спра́вочная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>správočnoje</b> izdánije; <b>správočnaja</b> kníga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reference book</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> engineering<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reference
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справочный.html>спра́вочный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:размер.html>разме́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>správočnyj</b> razmér</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reference size</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справочный.html>спра́вочный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:файл.html>файл</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>správočnyj</b> fajl</i> ― <span class="e-translation">help file</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справочный.html>спра́вочные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>да́нные</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>správočnyje</b> dánnyje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reference data</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> benchmark
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:справочный.html>спра́вочная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>цена́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>správočnaja</b> cená</i> ― <span class="e-translation">benchmark price</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спрашивать.html>спра́шивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sprášivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спросить.html>спроси́ть</a></b>)

<ol><li>to ask, to ask for, to inquire</li>
<li>to demand</li></ol>

***спровоцировавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спровоцировавший.html>спровоци́ровавший</a> (13810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спровоцировавший.html>спровоци́ровавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sprovocírovavšij</span>)
